<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Microsoft Cloud Strength Fuels Third Quarter Results </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>REDMOND, Wash. &#151; April</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;26, 2022 &#151; </B>Microsoft Corp. today announced the following results for the quarter ended
March&nbsp;31, 2022, as compared to the corresponding period of last fiscal year: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP)</FONT> </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP)</FONT> </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue and diluted earnings per share results include $(302)
million and $(0.03) of additional impact from unfavorable foreign exchange rate movement within the quarter and $111&nbsp;million and $(0.01) from Nuance, which closed on March&nbsp;4, 2022, neither of which were included in the forward-looking
guidance provided on January&nbsp;25, 2022. Additional details are provided in the Earnings Call Slides. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;Going forward, digital
technology will be the key input that powers the world&#146;s economic output,&#148; said Satya Nadella, chairman and chief executive officer of Microsoft. &#147;Across the tech stack, we are expanding our opportunity and taking share as we help
customers differentiate, build resilience, and do more with less.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;Continued customer commitment to our cloud platform and
strong sales execution drove better than expected commercial bookings growth of 28% and Microsoft Cloud revenue of $23.4&nbsp;billion, up 32% year over year,&#148; said Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief financial officer of Microsoft.

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Surface revenue increased 13% (up 18% CC) </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft returned $12.4&nbsp;billion to shareholders in the form of share repurchases and dividends in the third quarter of fiscal year 2022, an
increase of 25% compared to the third quarter of fiscal year 2021. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Business Outlook </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft will provide forward-looking guidance in connection with this quarterly earnings announcement on its earnings conference call and
webcast. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Quarterly Highlights, Product Releases, and Enhancements</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Every quarter Microsoft delivers hundreds of products, either as new releases, services, or enhancements to current products and services. These
releases are a result of significant research and development investments, made over multiple years, designed to help customers be more productive and secure and to deliver differentiated value across the cloud and the edge. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Here are the <U>major product releases and other highlights</U> for the quarter, organized by product categories, to help illustrate how we are
accelerating innovation across our businesses while expanding our market opportunities. </FONT></P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Environmental, Social, and Governance (ESG) </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">To better execute Microsoft&#146;s mission, we focus our Environmental, Social, and Governance (ESG) efforts where we can have the most positive
impact. To learn more about our latest initiatives and priorities, please visit our investor relations <U>ESG website</U>.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Webcast
Details </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Satya Nadella, chairman and chief executive officer, Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief financial officer, Alice
Jolla, chief accounting officer, Keith Dolliver, deputy general counsel, and Brett Iversen, general manager of investor relations, will host a conference call and webcast at 2:30 p.m. Pacific time (5:30 p.m. Eastern time) today to discuss details of
the company&#146;s performance for the quarter and certain forward-looking information. The session may be accessed at <U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">http://www.microsoft.com/en-us/investor</FONT></U>. The webcast will be available for replay
through the close of business on April&nbsp;26, 2023. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Definition </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>The India Supreme Court Decision Impact. </I>In March 2021, the India Supreme Court issued a decision on withholding taxes in the case of
Engineering Analysis Centre of Excellence Private Limited vs The Commissioner of Income Tax. Microsoft has historically paid India withholding taxes on software sales through distributor withholding and tax audit assessments in India. The India
Supreme Court ruled favorably for companies in 86 separate appeals, some dating back to 2012, holding that software sales are not subject to India withholding taxes. Although Microsoft was not a party to the appeals, Microsoft&#146;s software sales
in India were determined to be not subject to withholding taxes. Therefore, Microsoft recorded a net income tax benefit of $620&nbsp;million in the third quarter of fiscal year 2021 to reflect the results of the India Supreme Court decision
impacting fiscal year 1996 through fiscal year 2016. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft has provided <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial
measures related to the India Supreme Court decision to aid investors in better understanding our performance. Microsoft believes these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures assist investors by providing additional insight into
its operational performance and help clarify trends affecting its business. For comparability of reporting, management considers <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures in conjunction with GAAP financial results in evaluating
business performance. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented in this release should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with
GAAP. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Constant Currency </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Microsoft presents constant currency information to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding the effect of foreign currency rate fluctuations. To present this information, current and
comparative prior period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are converted into United States dollars using the average exchange rates from the comparative period rather than the actual exchange rates in
effect during the respective periods. All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. Microsoft has provided this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial information to aid investors in better
understanding our performance. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented in this release should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in
accordance with GAAP. </FONT></P>
</DIV></Center>
